  It is mandatory for all students to generate ABC ID by following process:

 1. Students can create ABC ID by visiting ab c.gov.in or through DigiLocker

4. Aadhar card verification is an essential process of registration. 20/01/23, 3:14‚ÄØpm - Anagha Mam: E-KUMBH is an AICTE initiative to unleash knowledge in multiple Bharatiya languages. The objective of AICTE is to provide outcome based Technical Education Books in different Indian Languages to the students and faculty members across all technical institutions in India. 
The books are available for various streams of Engineering like CIVIL, Computer Science, Electrical, Electronics & Communication, Mechanical and many more. All the students and faculties can take the benefit of the same by visiting the AICTE portal whose link is as mentioned below
https://ekumbh.aicte-india.org/index.php
The faculties and students needs to register first in the portal and then can download the available books as per their interests and requirements.

Smart India Hackathon 2023 is a nationwide initiative to provide students a platform to solve some of the pressing problems we face in our daily lives, and thus inculcate a culture of product innovation and a mindset of problem solving.

*Internal Hackathon Guidelines:*

1.	Each department will shortlist 8-10 Teams for Internal Hackathon which is scheduled on 28 September 2023.

4.	Each team should consist of *six* members, including at least *one female* team member.
5.	The choice of Problem statements could be from any theme or from the problem statement which is already published on the official SIH-2023 website.

Registration Page https://nasscom.in/techinnovate/

Event Overview:

The TechInnovate Challenge comprises five categories, each focusing on pressing issues:

Food for All: How can technology ensure no one goes to bed hungry? Present your game-changing solutions to revolutionize how we produce, distribute, and consume food.
Healthcare for All: More than ever, the world needs innovative solutions. Showcase your visionary ideas to provide accessible, affordable, and effective healthcare for every Indian.
Climate Change: Confronting one of the most significant challenges of our time, your innovations could be the key to preserving our planet. Unleash your creativity to combat climate change through groundbreaking technology.
Sustainability: Imagine a world where sustainable practices uplift communities from the grassroots. Share your ingenious tech-driven strategies to create lasting solutions that promote sustainability and economic well-being.
Education for All: Education empowers and transforms lives. Innovate ways to make quality education accessible to every corner of India, breaking down barriers and bridging gaps.
Key Dates:

Application Deadline: November 5th
Voting Period: November 13th - 16th
Winners Announcement: November 21st
Eligibility:

Participation is open to 3rd and final-year B-Tech and BSC students, making it an excellent opportunity for your students to showcase their talents.

We kindly request your support in encouraging your students to seize this opportunity.To learn more about the challenge and register, we invite your students to visit our registration page: https://nasscom.in/techinnovate/.

We look forward to witnessing your students' innovative solutions to the TechInnovate Challenge.

Best Regards,
Team Nasscom

23/02/24, 1:54‚ÄØpm - Sarala Mam Apsit: *Important Announcement Regarding AICTE-EduSkills Virtual Internship!!!*

As you know AICTE, Ministry of Education, Govt. of India is in the process of "Academic Bank of Credits" to support this initiative AICTE instructed us to implement a grading system in the virtual internship. So we are also implementing this from cohort 7 onwards.

 
Students need to appear for a final test after uploading all course completion certificates. This exam contains 30 Min 30 questions (MCQ). The questions relate to the courses students undergo during the internship.

 
Internship Grade Point (IGP)will be mentioned in the final internship certificate. So we are requested to inform all the students to read the course continent thoroughly for the final exam.
 

1. Number of Questions ‚Äì 30
2. Duration- 30 Min
3. Passing Mark- 30%
4. Each Question ‚Äì 1 Min
5. Back option will not work during the assessment 


If any student does not secure minimum 30% mark in the exam, then after 7 days students will get the last chance to clear the exam.  

*(Note:If any student is caught by our system doing bad practices then no more attempts will be given)*

27/02/24, 11:56‚ÄØpm - Shravani Kulkarni C Division Ap Shah: Respected Faculty , 
The Ojus Committee is deeply honoured and pleased to invite you to our college's pride - our annual cultural fest, OJUS Cultural 2k24. 

We would like to invite you for the faculty event of Ojus Cultural 2k24 on 28th February in the campus. 

üìçVenue: 008
üïôTime: 10am -12pm

The faculty events for Ojus Cultural 2k24 is as follows :
1) Relay Drawing Event : Teachers divide into teams, drawing parts of a picture in turns. Leaders guess the final drawing for points.
2) Whisper Challenge : Teachers in a line act out a movie or song to pass along. Last teacher acts out the final action or says the name aloud. 
3) Machli Game : Players start with "Ek machli" and "Paani mei gayi," then continue with "chapaak" in a sequence. They must repeat each phrase as many times as the sequence level, without breaking the pattern.
4) Ramp Walk : The winners of each game will walk on red carpet as a token of achievement.

We cordially invite you to join us for these events. Your presence will contribute to the success of the occasion. 

Thanking you, 
The Student Council
